    <script>
      /**
       * Inline Display Mode
       *
       * This script runs in head tag before CSS loads to apply
       * `deepai--light` or `deepai--dark` immediately, preventing
       * a flash of the wrong theme on first paint.
       */
      (function() {
        const STORAGE_KEY = 'deepai-display-mode';
        const stored = (function() {
          try {
            return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
          } catch (e) {
            return null;
          }
        })();

        let mode;
        if (stored === 'light' || stored === 'dark') {
          mode = stored;
        } else {
          const prefersDark = window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
          mode = prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light';
        }

        const html = document.documentElement;
        html.classList.remove('deepai--light', 'deepai--dark');
        html.classList.add('deepai--' + mode);
      })();
    </script>

            <span class="prompt-card__heading">Restore an old picture</span>
            <span class="prompt-card__text">
              First, ask me to upload an old family photo. After I upload the image, do the following—
First, acknowledge the photo I have uploaded, briefly and warmly state its potential, and then ask me two questions to guide the restoration.
What is the approximate era of this photo (e.g., 1920s, Victorian, 1950s)?
Are there any specific colors you would like me to consider for the clothing or background, or should I use my best historical judgment?
After I provide the information, use my answers to restore and colorize the photo, bringing it to life in a realistic, historically-appropriate, and high-quality image. The restoration should focus on—
Removing major blemishes, dust, or scratches.
Sharpening details that may have been lost over time.
Adding realistic color that reflects the era.
Present the newly restored and colorized image. After the image is created, briefly mention the key improvements you made (e.g., &quot;I focused on sharpening the lace details and chose a deep emerald green for the dress, popular in the late Victorian era&quot;). Finally, ask me if I&#x27;d like to try a different color palette or apply a specific artistic style (e.g., watercolor effect, sepia tone).
            </span>
          </div>

<p class="plain-text"><strong>Alumni Spotlight:&nbsp;</strong>Kayla Patterson, MS ’24 Computer Science</p><p class="su-intro-text">"I study human-computer interaction (HCI), because I want to understand how to think about people when it comes to developing technology. I’ve taken classes with James Landay, Michael Bernstein, and Christina Wodtke, and they just blew my mind with HCI."<br>Meet recent graduate, <a href="https://engineering.stanford.edu/spotlight/kayla-patterson">Kayla Patterson</a>, as she contemplates a new chapter in life</p></div>

            <div class="su-wysiwyg-text paragraph stanford-wysiwyg text-long label-hidden"><hr><h2>CS Degree Programs</h2><p>Our main educational goal is to prepare students for a rapidly changing world. Undergraduate students have the option of declaring a Bachelor of Science or a Minor in Computer Science. Graduate students have the opportunity to pursue a Master's or PhD degree in Computer Science. The Master's degree is a terminal professional degree. The PhD is for those who desire a research or teaching career.<br>&nbsp;</p><div class="media-entity-wrapper image">

            <div class="su-wysiwyg-text paragraph stanford-wysiwyg text-long label-hidden"><hr><h2>A Gateway to Opportunity &amp; Innovation</h2><p>Stanford Computer Science cultivates an expansive range of research opportunities and a renowned group of faculty. <div class="su-card__contents">
                  <h2>Diyi Yang on language, computers, and societal impact</h2>
                  <div class="su-card__superhead">We&#039;re in the News </div>
<p>Yang works on natural language processing, which combines math and theory to enable computers to communicate, through speech and text, in a human-like way. Specifically, she’s focused on making the technologies that power human-computer (and some human-human) communication more socially responsible.</p><p><a href="https://news.stanford.edu/stories/2024/11/diyi-yang-on-language-computers-and-societal-impact?utm_source=feedotter&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_campaign=int-11-11-2024&amp;utm_content=httpsnewsstanfordedustories202411diyiyangonlanguagecomputersandsocietalimpact&amp;mkt_tok=NjYwLVRKQy05ODQAAAGWv6lRrh8Gv2W4_5wHvI7Db1JxVbEMK_yA6id_124VWltvW3zhuAvSb6MNadrBoyZ2rxLLboCFgTj0FVzXXML-eyLzkbogYcauDdGn1yI">Read Assistant Professor Diyi Yang’s full interview</a> &nbsp;</p>
                  <a href="https://engineering.stanford.edu/school-news" class="su-link su-card__link su-link--action">
          More Stanford CS in the News
        </a>
      </div></article>

</div>
</div>

<div class="su-card__contents">
                  <h2>The future of AI coaching</h2>
                  <div class="su-card__superhead">We&#039;re in the News </div>
<p>A computer scientist bringing AI to the classroom and the gym looks ahead to a world where AI coaches help make us smarter … and healthier. Join host Russ Altman on this episode of <a href="https://engineering.stanford.edu/news/future-ai-coaching">The Future of Everything Podcast</a> and hear Professor James Landay share his thoughts on how AI is not just good at creating text and answering our questions, it can motivate us as a coach, and it can teach us as a tutor. It's the future of AI coaching.</p>
                  <a href="https://engineering.stanford.edu/school-news" class="su-link su-card__link su-link--action">
          More Stanford CS in the News
        </a>
      </div></article>

</div>

<div class="su-card__contents">
                  <h2>5 CS students receive Siebel Scholars Foundation scholarships</h2>
                  <div class="su-card__superhead">We&#039;re in the News</div>
<p>The Siebel Scholars Foundation has announced its 2026 scholarship recipients, including 19 Stanford students in business, bioengineering, computer science, and energy science. Five Siebel recipients are from the Computer Science department. Congratulations to Luciano Gonzalez, Georgious Mikos, Irawadee Thawornbut, Suzannah Wistreich, and Zhenyu Zhang.</p><p>Get the details <a href="https://news.stanford.edu/stories/2025/09/stanford-graduate-students-siebel-scholars?utm_content=httpsnewsstanfordedustories202509stanfordgraduatestudentssiebelscholars&amp;utm_source=feedotter&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_campaign=int-09-23-2025&amp;mkt_tok=NjYwLVRKQy05ODQAAAGdGtFoIcWUw3ElGPLksb6oPvdua-SoHwz2pAutTfntccBwyPrvOc8fY9KcLzFnOo8-GKoUQQoSmHhQ_LGsSnCE4PUfhrL7B4AKjDJfKsY">here</a></p>
                  <a href="https://engineering.stanford.edu/magazine" class="su-link su-card__link su-link--action">
          More Stanford CS in the News

</div>
      
</div>

  
<div class="su-card__contents">
                  <h2>Sanmi Koyejo, Assistant Professor Computer Science</h2>
                  <div class="su-card__superhead">Stories &amp; Voices</div>
<p>"I came to Stanford because it is among the strongest universities in my areas of interest: machine learning and AI. I’m interested in thinking about artificial intelligence in a rigorous way."</p>
                  <a href="https://engineering.stanford.edu/spotlight/sanmi-koyejo" class="su-link su-card__link su-link--action">
          Read Sanmi Koyejo&#039;s Story
        </a>
      </div></article>

<p>&nbsp;</p></div>

          <div class="ptype-stanford-media-caption">
<div class="ds-entity--paragraph ds-entity--stanford-media-caption">
  <div data-contextual-id="paragraph:root_parent_type=node&amp;root_parent=1726&amp;paragraph=4866:changed=1758755379&amp;ds_bundle=stanford_media_caption&amp;ds_view_mode=default&amp;langcode=en" data-contextual-token="RuhGbgVR0VCaZDRwVgyAIQTRpiASC5fuP24UKdo-RJU" data-drupal-ajax-container=""></div>
  



<figure  class="su-media ">

    <div class="su-media__wrapper ">            <div class="media-entity-wrapper image">
  
  




            <div class="media image field-media-image label-hidden">  <img loading="lazy" src="/sites/g/files/sbiybj28076/files/styles/card_1900x950/public/media/image/cs_site_home1_2025_0.jpg?h=6da36de0&amp;itok=8Rg6TgzV" width="1900" height="950" alt="Graduates at commencement 2025" />

              <div  class="layout__region layout__region--sidebar">
            <div class="ptype-stanford-wysiwyg paragraph paragraph--type--stanford-wysiwyg paragraph--view-mode--default">
          




            <div class="su-wysiwyg-text paragraph stanford-wysiwyg text-long label-hidden"><h3>"Working with students and faculty here is an absolutely amazing experience. What really impresses me is the conviction and drive of people here. They really care about the topics they work on. They want to bring value to people and they want to have an impact: to do good for humanity. It’s something very unique to Stanford. The speed at which you can exchange ideas was totally new to me when I came here and I love it."<br>&nbsp;</h3><p>- Christopher Hahn, Ph.D<br>Visiting Assistant Professor in the Computer Science Department at Stanford University and an Independent Research Group Leader at the CISPA Helmholtz Center for Information Security</p></div>
      
      </div>
